 varsh 2013 ke IPL-6 main spot fixing ke aarope ke baad pratibandhit kiye gaye team india ke tej gendbaaz es srisanth ab bhartiya cricket control board (bisisiai) ke bain ke khilaaf jate hue jaldi hi cricket khelte hue dikhaai de sakate hai
 Sreesanth has not played any cricket match since May 2013
 bisisiai ne unhen spot fixing kaa doshi paae jane ke baad un par aaajeevan pratibandh laga diya tha, lekin dilli ke trial court ne srisanth samet ajit chandila or ankit chavaan ko kisi bhi aapraadhik jurm kaa doshi nahin paaya tha
 In fact, Sreesanth had asked the BCCI for an NOC to play in Scotland, which was denied by the BCCI
 iske baad ab srisanth ne ernakulam cricket club kii ore se do divasiy first divizan match khilne kaa faisalaa kiya he
 Sreesanth also explained the reason behind this
 unhone kaha ki bisisiai ne un par lagaae aaajeevan pratibandh ko lekar koi patr jari nahin kiya he phir cricket sangh or ampire ise kyon maan rahe hai
 He told that when he was in Tihar Jail, he received only 90 days suspension letter from the BCCI
 dilli ke patiala court se anderworld don ke saath kisi bhi tarah ke conection na hone ke liye srisanth samet baaki khilaadiyon ko hari jhandi mili thi, lekin bisisiai ne uske baad hi saafe kar diya tha ki srisanth par aaajeevan pratibandh lagaaya gaya he
 The Anti Corruption Unit gave the names of these players to the BCCI and then the Board's Discipline Committee found them guilty

 The Ganesh festival is also going on at this time, so this fast gives the blessings of both Ganesha and Shri Hari

 This fast is extremely beneficial for those who want to attain child happiness or wealth
 is baar yah ekadshi 09 sitambar ko he

 yah sansadeey kshetra 1951 main hi astitv main aa gaya tha

 Bengali is the official language here
 iske saath hi hindi, urdu, marwari or angreji yahaan par aasaani se boli jaati he
 Political background: This seat was known as midnapore-jhargram in 1952
 1952 main yahaan se congress ke bharat laal tudu jite the
 In 1957 the name of this seat became Midnapore, this time also the Congress candidate won here
 1962 main congress ke gobind kumaar singhu saansad bane

 1971 main phir congress ke subodh chandra hansda yahaan se jeet gaye
 Sudhir Kumar Ghoshal of Bharatiya Lok Dal won in 1971
 1980 main sipiem ne is seat par kabja kar liya or narayan choube ko yahaan se vijay mili

 ' Mulayam Singh Yadav, the chief of the Samajwadi Party (SP), which had won a historic victory in the recent assembly elections in Uttar Pradesh, is busy exploring the possibility of a third front in the upcoming Lok Sabha elections
 tisare morche kii badaulat vah centre main ahm bhoomika adaa karnaa chaahate hai
 Despite the relatively good number of mps in the last two Lok Sabha elections, the grief of joining the central government has been haunting Mulayam
 isliye aagaamee loksabhaa chunaav main vah koi kor kasar nahin chhodana chaahate hai
 Mulayam feels that if his party wins more than 50 mps in the event of a third front in 2014, then his dream of becoming Prime Minister may get wings, but he also knows that this dream is largely to Uttar Pradesh That the work of the Akhilesh government can only be completed
 mulaayam ko pataa he ki uttar pradesh main sapa kii vidhansabha chunaav jaisi jeet tabhi doharaa paaegi jab akhilesh sarkaar kaa kaamkaaj behatar hoga or party kaaryakartaaon kii sarkaar main sunwaayee hogi
 So, he did not hesitate to show displeasure over the performance of his son-led government so far
 kaaryakartaaon kii sunwaayee na hone kii shikaayat or rajya sarkaar ke kuch mantriyon ke kaamkaaj se khafa mulaayam ne haal main mantriyon-vidhayakon kii baithak main bina kisi kaa naam liye ultimatum de diya ki behatar pradarshan na kar paane vaale or kaaryakartaaon kii andekhi karne vaale mantriyon ko bakhsha nahin jayega
 Mulayam, who is aiming for 60 Lok Sabha seats in the state, wants the SP government's image to be good among the people so that he can redeem its benefits in the Lok Sabha elections
 isliye vah lagaataar akhilesh sarkaar par jald se jald ghoshnaa patr ke vaade puraa karne kaa dabaav bana rahe hai
